   ## Custom Domains
   
  -`den domain` now makes the Sprite URL public and configures a Porkbun URL forward through `sesame`:

  +## Runtime Workflow Shortcuts

  +- `den domain myproject dev.example.com` uses ownership-based domain selection and defaults to DNS attachment

  +def _configured_domain_zones() -> dict[DomainProvider, list[str]]:
  +    return {

  +def _attach_cloudflare_dns_to_sprite(den_name: str, host: str, zone: str, *, proxied: bool) -> None:
  +    add_proc = _run_checked(
  +        fly_certs_add_command(den_name, host),
  +        capture_output=True,
  +        error_hint="Failed to attach the hostname to Fly.",
  +    )
  +    try:
  +        payload = json.loads(add_proc.stdout)
  +    except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
  +        raise CommandError("Fly returned malformed JSON while attaching the hostname.") from exc
  +
  +    try:
  +        records = parse_fly_dns_records(host, zone, payload, proxied=proxied)
  +        applied = upsert_cloudflare_dns_records(zone, records)
  +    except ValueError as exc:
  +        raise CommandError(str(exc)) from exc
  +
  +    typer.echo("  Cloudflare DNS:")
  +    for entry in applied:
  +        record = entry.get("record")
  +        if not isinstance(record, dict):
  +            continue
  +        typer.echo(f"    - {entry.get('action')}: {record['type']} {record['name']} -> {record['content']}")
  +
  +
  +def _attach_cloudflare_dns_to_railway(service: str, host: str, zone: str, *, proxied: bool, port: int | None) -> None:
  +    add_proc = _run_checked(
  +        railway_domain_attach_command(service, host, port=port),
  +        capture_output=True,
  +        error_hint="Failed to attach the hostname to Railway.",
  +    )
  +    try:
  +        payload = json.loads(add_proc.stdout)
  +    except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
  +        raise CommandError("Railway returned malformed JSON while attaching the hostname.") from exc
  +
  +    try:
  +        records = parse_railway_dns_records(host, zone, payload, proxied=proxied)
  +        applied = upsert_cloudflare_dns_records(zone, records)
  +    except ValueError as exc:
  +        raise CommandError(str(exc)) from exc
  +
  +    typer.echo("  Cloudflare DNS:")
  +    for entry in applied:
  +        record = entry.get("record")
  +        if not isinstance(record, dict):
  +            continue
  +        typer.echo(f"    - {entry.get('action')}: {record['type']} {record['name']} -> {record['content']}")

  +def resolve_custom_domain(
  +    host: str,
  +    provider_domains: Mapping[DomainProvider, Collection[str]],
  +) -> DomainMatch:
  +    """Resolve which provider owns a host by longest matching configured zone.
  +
  +    The domain authority should be selected by who actually holds the zone, not
  +    by a user preference. When multiple providers claim the same longest suffix,
  +    the result is treated as ambiguous and must be resolved explicitly.
  +    """
  +
  +    normalized = host.strip().strip(".").lower()
  +    labels = [label for label in normalized.split(".") if label]
  +    if len(labels) < 2:
  +        raise ValueError(f"invalid host: {host}")
  +
  +    matches: list[tuple[int, DomainProvider, str]] = []
  +    for provider, domains in provider_domains.items():
  +        for domain in domains:
  +            candidate = domain.strip().strip(".").lower()
  +            if not candidate:
  +                continue
  +            if normalized == candidate or normalized.endswith(f".{candidate}"):
  +                matches.append((len(candidate), provider, candidate))
  +
  +    if not matches:
  +        raise ValueError(
  +            f"Could not determine who holds {normalized}. Configure the owning zone in Cloudflare or sesame/Porkbun, or override the domain provider explicitly."
  +        )
  +
  +    matches.sort(key=lambda item: item[0], reverse=True)
  +    best_len = matches[0][0]
  +    best = [entry for entry in matches if entry[0] == best_len]
  +    unique = {(provider, zone) for _, provider, zone in best}
  +    if len(unique) != 1:
  +        providers = ", ".join(sorted(provider.value for provider, _ in unique))
  +        raise ValueError(f"Ambiguous domain ownership for {normalized}; matching zones found in: {providers}")
  +
  +    _, provider, zone = best[0]
  +    subdomain = None if normalized == zone else normalized[: -(len(zone) + 1)]
  +    return DomainMatch(provider=provider, zone=zone, subdomain=subdomain)
  +
  +
  +def build_sesame_url_forward_command(custom_domain: str, target_url: str, owned_domains: Collection[str]) -> list[str]:
  +    """Build the sesame command for a URL forward using resolved owned zones."""
  +
  +    match = resolve_custom_domain(custom_domain, {DomainProvider.sesame: owned_domains})
  +    command = [
  +        "domain",
  +        "add-url-forward",
  +        match.zone,
  +        "--location",
  +        target_url,
  +        "--type",
  +        "permanent",
  +        "--include-path",
  +        "yes",
  +    ]
  +    if match.subdomain:
  +        command.extend(["--subdomain", match.subdomain])
  +    return command
  +

  +def cloudflare_api_token() -> str | None:
  +    """Return a configured Cloudflare API token if one is available."""
  +
  +    for key in ("DEN_CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN", "CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN"):
  +        value = os.environ.get(key, "").strip()
  +        if value:
  +            return value
  +    return None

  +def resolve_flyctl_command() -> list[str]:
  +    """Resolve the Fly CLI command with local fallbacks."""
  +
  +    for candidate in ("flyctl", "fly"):
  +        path = shutil.which(candidate)
  +        if path:
  +            return [path]
  +
  +    fallback = Path.home() / ".fly" / "bin" / "flyctl"
  +    if fallback.is_file():
  +        return [str(fallback)]
  +    raise FileNotFoundError("flyctl executable not found")
  +
  +
  +def resolve_railway_command() -> list[str]:
  +    """Resolve the Railway CLI command with local fallbacks."""
  +
  +    path = shutil.which("railway")
  +    if path:
  +        return [path]
  +    fallback = Path.home() / ".local" / "share" / "mise" / "installs" / "railway" / "4.37.2" / "railway"
  +    if fallback.is_file():
  +        return [str(fallback)]
  +    raise FileNotFoundError("railway executable not found")
  +

  +def parse_railway_projects(payload: object) -> list[RailwayProjectSummary]:
  +    """Extract Railway projects from `railway list --json` output."""
  +
  +    if not isinstance(payload, list):
  +        raise ValueError("Railway list response was not a JSON array")
  +
  +    projects: list[RailwayProjectSummary] = []
  +    for row in payload:
  +        if not isinstance(row, Mapping):
  +            continue
  +        name = row.get("name")
  +        if not isinstance(name, str) or not name:
  +            continue
  +        project_id = row.get("id")
  +        if not isinstance(project_id, str) or not project_id:
  +            project_id = None
  +
  +        workspace_name: str | None = None
  +        workspace_obj = row.get("workspace")
  +        if isinstance(workspace_obj, Mapping):
  +            workspace_value = workspace_obj.get("name")
  +            if isinstance(workspace_value, str) and workspace_value:
  +                workspace_name = workspace_value
  +
  +        projects.append(
  +            RailwayProjectSummary(
  +                name=name,
  +                project_id=project_id,
  +                workspace_name=workspace_name,
  +            )
  +        )
  +    return projects
  +
  +
  +def extract_railway_linked_project_name(payload: object) -> str | None:
  +    """Best-effort extraction of the linked Railway project name from status JSON."""
  +
  +    if not isinstance(payload, Mapping):
  +        return None
  +
  +    project_obj = payload.get("project")
  +    if isinstance(project_obj, Mapping):
  +        project_name = project_obj.get("name")
  +        if isinstance(project_name, str) and project_name:
  +            return project_name
  +
  +    name = payload.get("name")
  +    has_project_shape = any(key in payload for key in ("environments", "services", "workspace"))
  +    if has_project_shape and isinstance(name, str) and name:
  +        return name
  +    return None
  +
  +
  +def parse_railway_dns_records(host: str, zone: str, payload: Mapping[str, object], *, proxied: bool = False) -> list[DnsRecord]:
  +    """Extract desired DNS records from Railway domain JSON payload."""
  +
  +    raw_records = payload.get("dnsRecords")
  +    if not isinstance(raw_records, list):
  +        status = payload.get("status")
  +        if isinstance(status, Mapping):
  +            raw_records = status.get("dnsRecords")
  +    if not isinstance(raw_records, list):
  +        raise ValueError("Railway domain response did not include dnsRecords")
  +
  +    normalized_zone = zone.strip().strip(".").lower()
  +    normalized_host = host.strip().strip(".").lower()
  +    desired_name = "@" if normalized_host == normalized_zone else normalized_host[: -(len(normalized_zone) + 1)]
  +
  +    records: list[DnsRecord] = []
  +    for row in raw_records:
  +        if not isinstance(row, Mapping):
  +            continue
  +        record_type = row.get("type")
  +        raw_name = row.get("name")
  +        target = row.get("target")
  +        value = row.get("value")
  +        content = target if isinstance(target, str) and target else value
  +        if not isinstance(record_type, str) or not isinstance(content, str) or not content:
  +            continue
  +        name = desired_name
  +        if isinstance(raw_name, str) and raw_name:
  +            normalized_name = raw_name.strip().strip(".").lower()
  +            if normalized_name == normalized_zone:
  +                name = "@"
  +            elif normalized_name.endswith(f".{normalized_zone}"):
  +                name = normalized_name[: -(len(normalized_zone) + 1)] or "@"
  +            else:
  +                name = normalized_name
  +        records.append(
  +            DnsRecord(
  +                type=record_type.upper(),
  +                name=name,
  +                content=content.rstrip("."),
  +                proxied=proxied if record_type.upper() in {"A", "AAAA", "CNAME"} else False,
  +            )
  +        )
  +
  +    if not records:
  +        raise ValueError("Railway domain response did not produce any DNS records")
  +    return records
  +
  +
  +def discover_cloudflare_domains() -> list[str]:
  +    """Discover Cloudflare-managed zones via the Cloudflare v4 API.
  +
  +    This is intentionally read-only discovery. If no token is configured or the
  +    API response is unavailable, return an empty list so callers can continue
  +    with other domain providers.
  +    """
  +
  +    token = cloudflare_api_token()
  +    if not token:
  +        return []
  +
  +    zones: list[str] = []
  +    page = 1
  +    while page <= 10:
  +        query = urllib.parse.urlencode({"page": page, "per_page": 50, "order": "name", "direction": "asc"})
  +        request = urllib.request.Request(
  +            f"https://api.cloudflare.com/client/v4/zones?{query}",
  +            headers={
  +                "Authorization": f"Bearer {token}",
  +                "Content-Type": "application/json",
  +            },
  +        )
  +        try:
  +            with urllib.request.urlopen(request, timeout=10) as response:
  +                payload = json.load(response)
  +        except Exception:
  +            return []
  +
  +        if not isinstance(payload, Mapping) or payload.get("success") is not True:
  +            return []
  +        result = payload.get("result")
  +        if not isinstance(result, list) or not result:
  +            break
  +
  +        for row in result:
  +            if not isinstance(row, Mapping):
  +                continue
  +            zone_name = row.get("name")
  +            if isinstance(zone_name, str) and zone_name:
  +                zones.append(zone_name.strip().strip(".").lower())
  +
  +        result_info = payload.get("result_info")
  +        if not isinstance(result_info, Mapping):
  +            break
  +        total_pages = result_info.get("total_pages")
  +        if not isinstance(total_pages, int) or page >= total_pages:
  +            break
  +        page += 1
  +
  +    return sorted(set(zones))
  +
  +
  +def _normalize_dns_name(name: str, zone: str) -> str:
  +    normalized = name.strip().rstrip(".").lower()
  +    normalized_zone = zone.strip().rstrip(".").lower()
  +    if normalized == normalized_zone:
  +        return "@"
  +    suffix = f".{normalized_zone}"
  +    if normalized.endswith(suffix):
  +        prefix = normalized[: -len(suffix)]
  +        return prefix.rstrip(".") or "@"
  +    return normalized
  +
  +
  +def build_cloudflare_dns_records(host: str, zone: str, dns_requirements: Mapping[str, object], *, proxied: bool = False) -> list[DnsRecord]:
  +    """Build desired Cloudflare DNS records from Fly-style dns_requirements."""
  +
  +    normalized_host = host.strip().strip(".").lower()
  +    normalized_zone = zone.strip().strip(".").lower()
  +    is_apex = normalized_host == normalized_zone
  +    records: list[DnsRecord] = []
  +
  +    ownership = dns_requirements.get("ownership")
  +    if isinstance(ownership, Mapping):
  +        ownership_name = ownership.get("name")
  +        ownership_value = ownership.get("app_value") or ownership.get("org_value")
  +        if isinstance(ownership_name, str) and isinstance(ownership_value, str):
  +            records.append(DnsRecord(type="TXT", name=_normalize_dns_name(ownership_name, normalized_zone), content=ownership_value))
  +
  +    if is_apex:
  +        a_values = dns_requirements.get("a")
  +        if isinstance(a_values, list):
  +            for value in a_values:
  +                if isinstance(value, str) and value:
  +                    records.append(DnsRecord(type="A", name="@",
  +                                             content=value, proxied=proxied))
  +        aaaa_values = dns_requirements.get("aaaa")
  +        if isinstance(aaaa_values, list):
  +            for value in aaaa_values:
  +                if isinstance(value, str) and value:
  +                    records.append(DnsRecord(type="AAAA", name="@",
  +                                             content=value, proxied=proxied))
  +    else:
  +        cname_value = dns_requirements.get("cname")
  +        if isinstance(cname_value, str) and cname_value:
  +            records.append(DnsRecord(type="CNAME", name=_normalize_dns_name(normalized_host, normalized_zone), content=cname_value.rstrip("."), proxied=proxied))
  +        else:
  +            a_values = dns_requirements.get("a")
  +            if isinstance(a_values, list):
  +                for value in a_values:
  +                    if isinstance(value, str) and value:
  +                        records.append(DnsRecord(type="A", name=_normalize_dns_name(normalized_host, normalized_zone), content=value, proxied=proxied))
  +            aaaa_values = dns_requirements.get("aaaa")
  +            if isinstance(aaaa_values, list):
  +                for value in aaaa_values:
  +                    if isinstance(value, str) and value:
  +                        records.append(DnsRecord(type="AAAA", name=_normalize_dns_name(normalized_host, normalized_zone), content=value, proxied=proxied))
  +
  +    seen: set[tuple[str, str, str, bool]] = set()
  +    deduped: list[DnsRecord] = []
  +    for record in records:
  +        key = (record.type, record.name, record.content, record.proxied)
  +        if key in seen:
  +            continue
  +        seen.add(key)
  +        deduped.append(record)
  +    return deduped
  +
  +
  +def parse_fly_dns_records(host: str, zone: str, payload: Mapping[str, object], *, proxied: bool = False) -> list[DnsRecord]:
  +    """Extract desired DNS records from Fly certificate JSON payload."""
  +
  +    requirements = payload.get("dns_requirements")
  +    if not isinstance(requirements, Mapping):
  +        raise ValueError("Fly certificate response did not include dns_requirements")
  +    records = build_cloudflare_dns_records(host, zone, requirements, proxied=proxied)
  +    if not records:
  +        raise ValueError("Fly certificate response did not produce any DNS records")
  +    return records
  +
  +
  +def upsert_cloudflare_dns_records(zone: str, records: Sequence[DnsRecord]) -> list[dict[str, object]]:
  +    """Create or update Cloudflare DNS records for a zone."""
  +
  +    token = cloudflare_api_token()
  +    if not token:
  +        raise ValueError("Cloudflare API token not configured")
  +
  +    zone_name = zone.strip().strip(".").lower()
  +
  +    def _request(path: str, *, method: str = "GET", payload: Mapping[str, object] | None = None) -> Mapping[str, object]:
  +        request = urllib.request.Request(
  +            f"https://api.cloudflare.com/client/v4{path}",
  +            method=method,
  +            headers={
  +                "Authorization": f"Bearer {token}",
  +                "Content-Type": "application/json",
  +            },
  +            data=json.dumps(payload).encode() if payload is not None else None,
  +        )
  +        with urllib.request.urlopen(request, timeout=15) as response:
  +            body = json.load(response)
  +        if not isinstance(body, Mapping) or body.get("success") is not True:
  +            raise ValueError(f"Cloudflare API request failed for {path}")
  +        return body
  +
  +    zones = _request(f"/zones?{urllib.parse.urlencode({'name': zone_name})}")
  +    result = zones.get("result")
  +    if not isinstance(result, list) or not result:
  +        raise ValueError(f"Cloudflare zone not found: {zone_name}")
  +    zone_row = result[0]
  +    if not isinstance(zone_row, Mapping):
  +        raise ValueError(f"Cloudflare zone lookup returned malformed result for {zone_name}")
  +    zone_id = zone_row.get("id")
  +    if not isinstance(zone_id, str) or not zone_id:
  +        raise ValueError(f"Cloudflare zone lookup did not include an id for {zone_name}")
  +
  +    applied: list[dict[str, object]] = []
  +    for record in records:
  +        fqdn = zone_name if record.name == "@" else f"{record.name}.{zone_name}"
  +        existing_resp = _request(
  +            f"/zones/{zone_id}/dns_records?{urllib.parse.urlencode({'type': record.type, 'name': fqdn})}"
  +        )
  +        existing_rows = existing_resp.get("result")
  +        payload: dict[str, object] = {
  +            "type": record.type,
  +            "name": fqdn,
  +            "content": record.content,
  +        }
  +        if record.type in {"A", "AAAA", "CNAME"}:
  +            payload["proxied"] = record.proxied
  +        if isinstance(existing_rows, list) and existing_rows:
  +            first = existing_rows[0]
  +            if not isinstance(first, Mapping):
  +                raise ValueError(f"Cloudflare DNS record lookup returned malformed result for {fqdn}")
  +            record_id = first.get("id")
  +            if not isinstance(record_id, str) or not record_id:
  +                raise ValueError(f"Cloudflare DNS record lookup did not include an id for {fqdn}")
  +            response = _request(f"/zones/{zone_id}/dns_records/{record_id}", method="PUT", payload=payload)
  +            action = "updated"
  +        else:
  +            response = _request(f"/zones/{zone_id}/dns_records", method="POST", payload=payload)
  +            action = "created"
  +        applied.append({"action": action, "record": payload, "response": response})
  +    return applied
  +
  +

  +        *,
  +        cwd=None,
  +        capture_output: bool = False,
  +        error_hint: str | None = None,
  +        input_text: str | None = None,

  +        del cwd, capture_output, error_hint, input_text

  +def test_deploy_railway_uses_railway_up(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:
  +    checked_calls: list[tuple[list[str], object | None, str | None]] = []
  +
  +    def fake_run_checked(
  +        cmd: list[str],
  +        *,
  +        cwd=None,
  +        capture_output: bool = False,
  +        error_hint: str | None = None,
  +        input_text: str | None = None,
  +    ) -> object:
  +        del capture_output, error_hint
  +        checked_calls.append((cmd, cwd, input_text))
  +        return object()
  +
  +    monkeypatch.setattr(cli, "_run_checked", fake_run_checked)
  +    monkeypatch.setattr(cli, "_command_exists", lambda name: False)

  +def test_list_railway_shows_den_projects(monkeypatch) -> None:

  +        cmd: list[str],
  +        *,
  +        cwd=None,
  +        capture_output: bool = False,

  +        del cwd, capture_output, error_hint, input_text

  +def test_destroy_railway_deletes_matching_linked_project(monkeypatch) -> None:
  +    checked_calls: list[list[str]] = []
  +
  +    def fake_run_checked(
  +        cmd: list[str],
  +        *,
  +        cwd=None,
  +        capture_output: bool = False,
  +        error_hint: str | None = None,
  +        input_text: str | None = None,
  +    ) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
  +        del cwd, capture_output, error_hint, input_text
  +        checked_calls.append(cmd)
  +        if cmd == cli.railway_status_command():
  +            payload = {"project": {"name": "den-myproject"}}
  +            return subprocess.CompletedProcess(cmd, 0, stdout=json.dumps(payload), stderr="")
  +        return subprocess.CompletedProcess(cmd, 0, stdout="{}", stderr="")
  +
  +    monkeypatch.setattr(cli, "_run_checked", fake_run_checked)
  +
  +    result = runner.invoke(cli.app, ["destroy", "myproject", "--runtime", "railway"], input="y\n")
  +
  +    assert result.exit_code == 0
  +    assert checked_calls == [
  +        cli.railway_status_command(),
  +        cli.railway_delete_command("den-myproject"),
  +    ]

  +        cwd=None,
  +        capture_output: bool = False,
  +        error_hint: str | None = None,
  +        input_text: str | None = None,
  +    ) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
  +        del cwd, capture_output, error_hint, input_text
  +        payload = {"project": {"name": "den-other"}}
  +        return subprocess.CompletedProcess(cmd, 0, stdout=json.dumps(payload), stderr="")
  +
  +    monkeypatch.setattr(cli, "_run_checked", fake_run_checked)
  +
  +    result = runner.invoke(cli.app, ["destroy", "myproject", "--runtime", "railway"], input="y\n")
  +
  +    assert result.exit_code == 1
  +    assert isinstance(result.exception, cli.CommandError)
  +    assert "linked project is den-other" in str(result.exception)
  +

  --- /dev/null
  +++ b/.claude/projects/-home-diogenes-Projects-den/memory/feedback_provider_abstraction.md
  @@ -0,0 +1,11 @@
  +---
  +name: provider abstraction is premature
  +description: User considers provider abstraction difficult and lower priority than connectivity, visibility, and test coverage
  +type: feedback
  +---
  +
  +Don't push for provider abstraction as the top priority. Provisioning is hard and the current Sprite-only path works.
  +
  +**Why:** The user sees more value in richer visibility (list/status showing domains, access methods, connectivity state) and multiple access methods (Tailscale, zrok, Coder, Zellij) than in abstracting the provider layer.
  +
  +**How to apply:** Focus on making the existing Sprite provider richer (better list output, connectivity options) and improving test coverage before trying to extract a generic Provider protocol.

  diff --git a/.claude/projects/-home-diogenes-Projects-den/memory/project_connectivity_vision.md b/.claude/projects/-home-diogenes-Projects-den/memory/project_connectivity_vision.md
  new file mode 100644
  index 0000000..bba4662
  --- /dev/null
  +++ b/.claude/projects/-home-diogenes-Projects-den/memory/project_connectivity_vision.md
  @@ -0,0 +1,19 @@
  +---
  +name: den connectivity and access vision
  +description: User's vision for how dens should be accessed — multiple connectivity layers (Tailscale, zrok, Coder, Zellij) not just Sprite console
  +type: project
  +---
  +
  +Den should support multiple ways to connect to and work in remote environments beyond just `sprite console`:
  +
  +- **Tailscale**: dens on your tailnet so you can SSH directly
  +- **zrok**: dens available for SSH without tailnet membership
  +- **Coder**: `den connect <name> --web` or `den work <name>` opens a full Coder dev environment on the sprite machine with IDE, terminal, etc.
  +- **Crush/agent**: agent sessions running inside dens
  +- **Zellij**: serve a remote terminal session over the web (zellij has a server mode)
  +
  +The user wants `den list` / `den status` to show not just names but: which machines are available, what domains they're on, whether they're reachable via tailnet/zrok/coder.
  +
  +**Why:** The goal is "open a remote machine and get some work done" from any device/context — phone, laptop, web browser, terminal. Multiple access methods serve different contexts.
  +
  +**How to apply:** When building connectivity features, don't hardcode a single access method. The provider abstraction should cover environment lifecycle, but *access methods* (Tailscale, zrok, Coder, Zellij-serve) are orthogonal and composable. `den list` should surface which access methods are available per den.

  +# Den CLI Public API Documentation
  +
  +This document provides an overview of the public APIs, functions, classes, and interfaces available within the `den_cli` package.
  +
  +## Module: `den_cli.core`
  +
  +This module contains core logic for managing Den environments, including name normalization, Sprite command building, project marker detection, setup inference, and domain utilities.
  +
  +### Classes & Data Structures (`den_cli.core`)
  +
  +#### DenPeer
  +Represents a minimal view of a Den peer extracted from a Tailscale status payload.
  +```python
  +@dataclass(frozen=True)
  +class DenPeer:
  +    host_name: str
  +    ip: str
  +    online: bool
  +```
  +
  +#### ProjectMarkers
  +A data structure holding boolean flags indicating the presence of specific project files, used to infer a reproducible den setup.
  +```python
  +@dataclass(frozen=True)
  +class ProjectMarkers:
  +    has_package_json: bool
  +    has_bun_lock: bool
  +    has_pyproject: bool
  +    has_cargo_toml: bool
  +    has_dockerfile: bool
  +    has_containerfile: bool
  +    has_mise_toml: bool
  +    has_flox_toml: bool
  +    has_helm_chart: bool
  +    has_nix_flake: bool
  +    has_shell_nix: bool
  +    has_guix_manifest: bool
  +    has_guix_channels: bool
  +```
  +
  +#### InferredDenSetup
  +A normalized plan for a Den setup, produced from repository markers before Dhall rendering.
  +```python
  +@dataclass(frozen=True)
  +class InferredDenSetup:
  +    name: str
  +    backend: Literal["nix", "guix"]
  +    dockerfile: str | None
  +    nix_packages: tuple[str, ...]
  +    guix_packages: tuple[str, ...]
  +    environment: tuple[tuple[str, str], ...]
  +    reasons: tuple[str, ...]
  +```
  +
  +#### InferredRunCommand
  +Represents the best-effort command Den can launch for live development on a sprite.
  +```python
  +@dataclass(frozen=True)
  +class InferredRunCommand:
  +    command: tuple[str, ...]
  +    reasons: tuple[str, ...]
  +```
  +
  +#### SpriteUrlInfo
  +Contains parsed information from a Sprite URL output, including the URL, host, and domain.
  +```python
  +@dataclass(frozen=True)
  +class SpriteUrlInfo:
  +    url: str
  +    host: str
  +    domain: str
  +```
  +
  +### Functions (`den_cli.core`)
  +
  +#### normalize_den_name
  +Ensures human-facing Den names adhere to the Sprite naming convention by prefixing with 'den-' if necessary. The function `normalize_den_name` is idempotent.
  +```python
  +def normalize_den_name(name: str) -> str:
  +    """Ensure human-facing den names are normalized to the Sprite naming convention."""
  +
  +    return name if name.startswith("den-") else f"den-{name}"
  +```
  +
  +#### short_den_name
  +Removes the canonical 'den-' prefix for display-oriented output from a `name`.
  +```python
  +def short_den_name(name: str) -> str:
  +    """Drop the canonical den prefix for display-oriented output."""
  +
  +    return name[4:] if name.startswith("den-") else name
  +```
  +
  +#### sprite_org
  +Returns the preferred Sprite organization from environment variables (`DEN_SPRITE_ORG` or `SPRITE_ORG`).
  +```python
  +def sprite_org() -> str | None:
  +    """Return the preferred Sprite org from den-specific or upstream env vars."""
  +
  +    for key in ("DEN_SPRITE_ORG", "SPRITE_ORG"):
  +        value = os.environ.get(key, "").strip()
  +        if value:
  +            return value
  +    return None
  +```
  +
  +#### sprite_command
  +Constructs a Sprite CLI command, optionally including organization and normalized `sprite_name` context.
  +```python
  +def sprite_command(*args: str, sprite_name: str | None = None) -> list[str]:
  +    """Build a Sprite CLI command with optional org and normalized sprite context."""
  +
  +    command = ["sprite"]
  +    org = sprite_org()
  +    if org:
  +        command.extend(["-o", org])
  +    if sprite_name:
  +        command.extend(["-s", normalize_den_name(sprite_name)])
  +    command.extend(args)
  +    return command
  +```
  +
  +#### sprite_exec_command
  +Builds the Sprite argv for a non-interactive command execution within a Den specified by `name`.
  +```python
  +def sprite_exec_command(name: str, command: Sequence[str]) -> list[str]:
  +    """Build the Sprite argv for a non-interactive command execution."""
  +
  +    return sprite_command("exec", "--", *command, sprite_name=name)
  +```
  +
  +#### sprite_tty_exec_command
  +Builds the Sprite argv for a long-running interactive TTY session within a Den specified by `name`.
  +```python
  +def sprite_tty_exec_command(name: str, command: Sequence[str]) -> list[str]:
  +    """Build the Sprite argv for a long-running interactive TTY session."""
  +
  +    return sprite_command("exec", "--tty", "--", *command, sprite_name=name)
  +```
  +
  +#### sprite_use_command
  +Builds the Sprite argv for binding the current directory to a specified Sprite identified by `name`.
  +```python
  +def sprite_use_command(name: str) -> list[str]:
  +    """Build the Sprite argv for binding the current directory to a sprite."""
  +
  +    command = ["sprite"]
  +    org = sprite_org()
  +    if org:
  +        command.extend(["-o", org])
  +    command.extend(["use", normalize_den_name(name)])
  +    return command
  +```
  +
  +#### sprite_logs_command
  +Builds the Sprite argv for session listing or attaching to a specific Den session.
  +```python
  +def sprite_logs_command(name: str, selector: str | None = None, *, list_only: bool = False) -> list[str]:
  +    """Build the Sprite argv for session listing or attachment."""
  +
  +    if list_only:
  +        return sprite_command("sessions", "list", sprite_name=name)
  +    if selector:
  +        return sprite_command("attach", selector, sprite_name=name)
  +    return sprite_command("attach", sprite_name=name)
  +```
  +
  +#### sprite_checkpoint_create_command
  +Builds the Sprite argv for checkpoint creation with a stable `comment` tag for the Den `name`.
  +```python
  +def sprite_checkpoint_create_command(name: str, comment: str) -> list[str]:
  +    """Build the Sprite argv for checkpoint creation with a stable comment tag."""
  +
  +    return sprite_command("checkpoint", "create", "--comment", comment, sprite_name=name)
  +```
  +
  +#### sprite_restore_command
  +Builds the Sprite argv for restoring a checkpoint to a specific `version_id` for the Den `name`.
  +```python
  +def sprite_restore_command(name: str, version_id: str) -> list[str]:
  +    """Build the Sprite argv for restoring a checkpoint version."""
  +
  +    return sprite_command("restore", version_id, sprite_name=name)
  +```
  +
  +#### make_sprite_redeploy_comment
  +Generates a unique checkpoint comment using the Den `name` and a `nonce` that `den_cli` can use to search for after creation, typically for redeployment.
  +```python
  +def make_sprite_redeploy_comment(name: str, nonce: str) -> str:
  +    """Create a unique checkpoint comment that den can search for after creation."""
  +
  +    return f"den-redeploy:{normalize_den_name(name)}:{nonce}"
  +```
  +
  +#### detect_project_markers
  +Collects coarse repository signals from a given `root` path, populating a `ProjectMarkers` object, used by setup inference heuristics.
  +```python
  +def detect_project_markers(root: Path) -> ProjectMarkers:
  +    """Collect coarse repository signals used by the setup inference heuristics."""
  +
  +    return ProjectMarkers(
  +        has_package_json=(root / "package.json").is_file(),
  +        has_bun_lock=(root / "bun.lock").is_file() or (root / "bun.lockb").is_file(),
  +        has_pyproject=(root / "pyproject.toml").is_file(),
  +        has_cargo_toml=(root / "Cargo.toml").is_file(),
  +        has_dockerfile=(root / "Dockerfile").is_file(),
  +        has_containerfile=(root / "Containerfile").is_file(),
  +        has_mise_toml=(root / "mise.toml").is_file(),
  +        has_flox_toml=(root / "flox.toml").is_file(),
  +        has_helm_chart=(root / "Chart.yaml").is_file() or (root / "charts").is_dir(),
  +        has_nix_flake=(root / "flake.nix").is_file(),
  +        has_shell_nix=(root / "shell.nix").is_file(),
  +        has_guix_manifest=(root / "guix" / "manifest.scm").is_file(),
  +        has_guix_channels=(root / "guix" / "channels.scm").is_file(),
  +    )
  +```
  +
  +#### infer_den_setup
  +Infers a typed `InferredDenSetup` plan based on repository markers in the `root` path, choosing a backend and default packages.
  +```python
  +def infer_den_setup(root: Path) -> InferredDenSetup:
  +    """Infer a typed den setup plan from repository markers.\n\n    This is the pure decision layer behind `den setup`: it chooses a backend,
  +    selects default package sets, and prepares environment metadata that will
  +    later be rendered into `den.dhall`.
  +    """
  +
  +    markers = detect_project_markers(root)
  +
  +    backend, reasons = _infer_backend(markers)
  +    name = root.name or "workspace"
  +    dockerfile = None
  +    if markers.has_dockerfile:
  +        dockerfile = "Dockerfile"
  +    elif markers.has_containerfile:
  +        dockerfile = "Containerfile"
  +
  +    nix_packages = _infer_nix_packages(markers)
  +    guix_packages = _infer_guix_packages(markers)
  +    environment_rows: list[tuple[str, str]] = [
  +        ("DEN_NAME", normalize_den_name(name)),
  +        ("DEN_BACKEND", backend),
  +    ]
  +    if dockerfile is not None:
  +        environment_rows.append(("DEN_DOCKERFILE", dockerfile))
  +
  +    return InferredDenSetup(
  +        name=name,
  +        backend=backend,
  +        dockerfile=dockerfile,
  +        nix_packages=nix_packages,
  +        guix_packages=guix_packages,
  +        environment=tuple(environment_rows),
  +        reasons=reasons,
  +    )
  +```
  +
  +#### infer_run_command
  +Determines a best-effort `InferredRunCommand` that the Den can launch for live development, based on project markers in the `root` path.
  +```python
  +def infer_run_command(root: Path) -> InferredRunCommand:
  +    """Best-effort command den can launch for live development on a sprite."""
  +
  +    # ... (truncated)
  +```

  +#### render_den_dhall
  +Transforms an `InferredDenSetup` plan into a concrete `den.dhall` expression string, using Dhall templates located in `dhall_dir`.
  +```python
  +def render_den_dhall(config: InferredDenSetup, dhall_dir: Path) -> str:
  +    """Render an inferred setup plan into a concrete `den.dhall` expression."""
  +
  +    backend_expr = "Types.Backend.Nix" if config.backend == "nix" else "Types.Backend.Guix"
  +    dockerfile_expr = _optional_text(config.dockerfile)
  +    nix_expr = _render_nix_config(config.nix_packages) if conf... (truncated)
  +```
  +
  +#### parse_sprite_url
  +Parses the URL from a Sprite CLI output (`output`) containing 'URL: ...' and 'Auth: ...'.
  +```python
  +def parse_sprite_url(output: str) -> str | None:
  +    """Extract the public Sprite URL from output like `URL: https://foo.sprites.app\nAuth: public`."""
  +
  +    for line in output.splitlines():
  +        if line.startswith("URL:"):
  +            return urlparse(line[4:].strip())._replace(scheme="https").geturl()
  +    return None
  +```
  +
  +#### parse_sprite_url_info
  +Parses detailed URL information into a `SpriteUrlInfo` object from Sprite CLI `output`.
  +```python
  +def parse_sprite_url_info(output: str) -> SpriteUrlInfo | None:
  +    """Parse detailed URL info from Sprite output.\n\n    Example output:\n    URL: https://den-myproject.sprites.app\n    Auth: public
  +    """
  +    url = parse_sprite_url(output)
  +    if url is None:
  +        return None
  +    parsed = urlparse(url)
  +    return SpriteUrlInfo(url=url, host=parsed.netloc, domain=parsed.hostname or "")
  +```
  +
  +#### find_checkpoint_version_in_api_output
  +Extracts a checkpoint version ID from a JSON API `payload` (list or nested structure) given a specific `comment`.
  +```python
  +def find_checkpoint_version_in_api_output(payload: str, comment: str) -> str | None:
  +    """Find a checkpoint version ID by comment in Sprite API output.\n\n    The payload is expected to be a JSON list of checkpoints or a dict containing
  +    a list of checkpoints under a 'data' key.
  +    """
  +    data = json.loads(payload)
  +    if not isinstance(data, list) and isinstance(data, Mapping) and "data" in data:
  +        data = data["data"]
  +
  +    for item in data:
  +        if isinstance(item, Mapping) and item.get("comment") == comment:
  +            return item.get("id") or item.get("version")  # 'id' for flat list, 'version' for nested
  +    return None
  +```
  +
  +#### find_checkpoint_version_in_list_output
  +Extracts a checkpoint `version_id` from plain-text `sprite checkpoint list` `output` given a specific `comment`.
  +```python
  +def find_checkpoint_version_in_list_output(output: str, comment: str) -> str | None:
  +    """Find a checkpoint version ID by comment in `sprite checkpoint list` output.\n\n    Expected output format: `version_id  comment  timestamp\n`
  +    """
  +    for line in output.splitlines():
  +        parts = line.strip().split("  ", 1) # Split only on the first two spaces
  +        if len(parts) == 2 and parts[1].startswith(comment):
  +            return parts[0]
  +    return None
  +```
  +
  +#### split_custom_domain
  +Splits a full `host` (e.g., `app.dev.example.com`) into its `zone` and `subdomain` parts based on a list of `owned_domains`, preferring the longest match.
  +```python
  +def split_custom_domain(host: str, owned_domains: Collection[str]) -> tuple[str, str | None]:
  +    """Splits a full custom domain host into its zone and subdomain parts.\n\n    Example: host='app.dev.example.com', owned_domains=['example.com', 'dev.example.com']\n    Returns: ('dev.example.com', 'app')\n\n    It prefers the longest matching owned domain suffix.
  +    """
  +    longest_zone = ""
  +    for domain in owned_domains:
  +        if host.endswith(domain) and len(domain) > len(longest_zone):
  +            longest_zone = domain
  +
  +    if not longest_zone:
  +        raise ValueError(f"Host {host} does not match any owned domains.")
  +
  +    # If host is exactly the zone, there is no subdomain.
  +    if host == longest_zone:
  +        return longest_zone, None
  +
  +    # Subdomain is the part before the longest_zone, excluding the dot
  +    subdomain = host[: -len(longest_zone)].rstrip(".")
  +    return longest_zone, subdomain or None # subdomain can be empty if it's just the zone.
  +```
  +
  +#### resolve_sesame_command
  +Determines the path to the `sesame` executable, prioritizing `SESAME_COMMAND` environment variable, then local build, then system PATH. Raises `FileNotFoundError` if not found.
  +```python
  +def resolve_sesame_command() -> list[str]:
  +    """Resolve the sesame CLI command path.\n\n    This allows us to bundle sesame or use a path from env vars.
  +    """
  +    if command := os.environ.get("SESAME_COMMAND"):
  +        return shlex.split(command)
  +    local_sesame = Path(__file__).parent.parent.parent / "bin" / "sesame"
  +    if local_sesame.is_file():
  +        return [str(local_sesame)]
  +    if shutil.which("sesame"):
  +        return ["sesame"]
  +    raise FileNotFoundError("sesame executable not found")
  +```
  +
  +#### discover_porkbun_domains_from_sesame_config
  +Discovers domains configured with Porkbun credentials from `sesame` configuration files (`SECRETS_FILE`).
  +```python
  +def discover_porkbun_domains_from_sesame_config() -> list[str]:
  +    """Discover domains configured with Porkbun credentials in sesame's sops config.\n\n    This is a fallback if `sesame domain list` fails or isn't available.
  +    """
  +    if not SECRETS_FILE.is_file():
  +        return []
  +    try:
  +        with open(SECRETS_FILE, "rb") as f:
  +            data = tomllib.load(f)
  +    except Exception:
  +        return []
  +
  +    domains: list[str] = []
  +    for account_data in data.get("porkbun_accounts", []):
  +        if isinstance(account_data, Mapping) and "domains" in account_data:
  +            account_domains = account_data["domains"]
  +            if isinstance(account_domains, list):
  +                for domain in account_domains:
  +                    if isinstance(domain, str):
  +                        domains.append(domain)
  +    return sorted(list(dict.fromkeys(domains))) # Deduplicate and sort
  +```
  +
  +#### extract_den_peers
  +Extracts `DenPeer` information from a Tailscale status JSON `tailscale_status_json` payload.
  +```python
  +def extract_den_peers(tailscale_status_json: str) -> list[DenPeer]:
  +    """Extract den peers from a tailscale status payload."""
  +
  +    parsed = json.loads(tailscale_status_json)
  +    peers: list[DenPeer] = []
  +    for peer in parsed.get("Peer", {}).values():
  +        if "den" in peer.get("HostName", ""):
  +            peers.append(
  +                DenPeer(
  +                    host_name=peer["HostName"],
  +                    ip=peer["TailscaleIPs"][0],
  +                    online=peer["Online"],
  +                )
  +            )
  +    return peers
  +```
  +
  +## Module: `den_cli.mcp_server`
  +
  +This module implements the FastMCP server for Den, exposing workflow-oriented tools for provisioning, operating, and diagnosing Dens.
  +
  +### Interfaces (`den_cli.mcp_server`)
  +
  +#### StepResult (TypedDict)
  +Represents the outcome of a single step within an MCP workflow.
  +```python
  +class StepResult(TypedDict):
  +    step: str
  +    command: list[str]
  +    cwd: str
  +    ok: bool
  +    exit_code: int | None
  +    timed_out: bool
  +    duration_ms: int
  +    stdout: str
  +    stderr: str
  +```
  +
  +#### WorkflowError (TypedDict)
  +Describes an error encountered during an MCP workflow, providing details about the failure and possible remediation.
  +```python
  +class WorkflowError(TypedDict):
  +    kind: str
  +    message: str
  +    failing_step: str
  +    command: list[str]
  +    exit_code: int | None
  +    timed_out: bool
  +    stdout: str
  +    stderr: str
  +    remediation: list[str]
  +```
  +
  +### MCP Tools (`den_cli.mcp_server`)
  +These functions are exposed as public API endpoints by the FastMCP server.
  +
  +#### provision_den
  +Executes a comprehensive workflow to provision a new Den, including prerequisites checks, Sprite creation, and optional custom domain setup.
  +```python
  +@mcp.tool
  +def provision_den(
  +    name: str,
  +    backend: Literal["nix", "guix"] = "nix",
  +    tailscale_authkey: str | None = None,
  +    custom_domain: str | None = None,
  +) -> dict[str, Any]:
  +    """Provision workflow: prerequisites + spawn + optional domain in one call."""
  +    del tailscale_authkey
  +    steps: list[StepResult] = []
  +    den_name = normalize_den_name(name)
  +
  +    for cmd in ("sprite",):
  +        exists = _command_exists(cmd)
  +        if not exists:
  +            return _result(
  +                "provision_den",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error={
  +                    "kind": "missing_dependency",
  +                    "message": f"Required command not found: {cmd}",
  +                    "failing_step": "preflight",
  +                    "command": ["command", "-v", cmd],
  +                    "exit_code": None,
  +                    "timed_out": False,
  +                    "stdout": "",
  +                    "stderr": f"{cmd} is not on PATH",
  +                    "remediation": [
  +                        "Install the Sprite CLI and authenticate with Fly.",
  +                        "Retry provision_den after sprite list succeeds.",
  +                    ],
  +                },
  +            )
  +
  +    try:
  +        sesame_cmd = _sesame_command()
  +    except FileNotFoundError:
  +        sesame_cmd = []
  +    if custom_domain and not sesame_cmd:
  +        return _result(
  +            "provision_den",
  +            False,
  +            steps=steps,
  +            error={
  +                "kind": "missing_dependency",
  +                "message": "sesame is required when custom_domain is provided",
  +                "failing_step": "preflight",
  +                "command": ["sesame", "--help"],
  +                "exit_code": None,
  +                "timed_out": False,
  +                "stdout": "",
  +                "stderr": "sesame is not on PATH and no local build was found",
  +                "remediation": [
  +                    "Build or install sesame.",
  +                    "Or omit custom_domain and configure the domain later.",
  +                ],
  +            },
  +        )
  +
  +    if not PROJECT_DIR.is_dir():
  +        return _result(
  +            "provision_den",
  +            False,
  +            steps=steps,
  +            error={
  +                "kind": "missing_project",
  +                "message": f"den project directory not found: {PROJECT_DIR}",
  +                "failing_step": "preflight",
  +                "command": ["test", "-d", str(PROJECT_DIR)],
  +                "exit_code": None,
  +                "timed_out": False,
  +                "stdout": "",
  +                "stderr": "Project directory missing",
  +                "remediation": [
  +                    "Clone or restore ~/Projects/den.",
  +                    "Run the command again after restoring project files.",
  +                ],
  +            },
  +        )
  +
  +    sprite_auth = _run_step("sprite_list", sprite_command("list"), cwd=PROJECT_DIR, timeout_s=20)
  +    steps.append(sprite_auth)
  +    if not sprite_auth["ok"]:
  +        return _result(
  +            "provision_den",
  +            False,
  +            steps=steps,
  +            error=_build_error(
  +                sprite_auth,
  +                "Sprite authentication check failed.",
  +                [
  +                    "Run: sprite login",
  +                    "Verify you can run: sprite list",
  +                    "Retry provision_den after successful login",
  +                ],
  +            ),
  +        )
  +
  +    command_plan: list[tuple[str, list[str], Path | None, int, str | None]] = [
  +        ("sprite_create", sprite_command("create", "-skip-console"), PROJECT_DIR, 180, f"{den_name}\n"),
  +    ]
  +
  +    for step_name, command, cwd, timeout_s, input_text in command_plan:
  +        step = _run_step(step_name, command, cwd=cwd, timeout_s=timeout_s, input_text=input_text)
  +        steps.append(step)
  +        if not step["ok"]:
  +            return _result(
  +                "provision_den",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error=_build_error(
  +                    step,
  +                    f"Provisioning failed at {step_name}",
  +                    [
  +                        "Inspect stderr/stdout in this error payload.",
  +                        "Fix auth or provider state, then retry.",
  +                        f"Backend selection ({backend}) is informational in the current Sprite flow.",
  +                    ],
  +                ),
  +            )
  +
  +    if custom_domain:
  +        public_step = _run_step(
  +            "sprite_url_public",
  +            sprite_command("url", "update", "--auth", "public", sprite_name=den_name),
  +            cwd=PROJECT_DIR,
  +            timeout_s=30,
  +        )
  +        steps.append(public_step)
  +        if not public_step["ok"]:
  +            return _result(
  +                "provision_den",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error=_build_error(
  +                    public_step,
  +                    "Provision succeed... (truncated)
  +```
  +
  +#### operate_den
  +Performs lifecycle operations on a Den, such as listing, creating, destroying, getting status, or managing domains. It routes to different sub-workflows based on the `action` parameter.
  +```python
  +@mcp.tool
  +def operate_den(
  +    action: Literal[
  +        "list",
  +        "create",
  +        "destroy",
  +        "status",
  +        "domain",
  +        "redeploy",  # Not currently supported by MCP server.
  +        "logs",  # Not currently supported by MCP server.
  +    ],
  +    name: str | None = None,
  +    # Additional arguments for specific actions
  +    confirm_destroy: bool = False,
  +    tailscale_authkey: str | None = None,
  +    custom_domain: str | None = None,
  +    target_url: str | None = None,
  +) -> dict[str, Any]:
  +    """Operate a den lifecycle action.\n\n    This is the primary tool call for managing dens. The `action` parameter
  +    determines the specific operation, and other parameters provide context
  +    for that action. See the documentation for `den_cli.cli` for user-facing
  +    equivalents.
  +    """
  +    steps: list[StepResult] = []
  +
  +    if action == "list":
  +        list_step = _run_step("sprite_list", sprite_command("list", "-prefix", "den-"), cwd=PROJECT_DIR, timeout_s=30)
  +        steps.append(list_step)
  +        if not list_step["ok"]:
  +            return _result(
  +                "operate_den_list",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error=_build_error(
  +                    list_step,
  +                    "Failed to list dens.",
  +                    ["Check sprite CLI authentication.", "Run `sprite list` manually."],
  +                ),
  +            )
  +        dens = [
  +            line.strip() for line in list_step["stdout"].splitlines() if line.strip().startswith("den-")
  +        ]
  +        return _result(
  +            "operate_den_list",
  +            True,
  +            steps=steps,
  +            data={
  +                "action": "list",
  +                "count": len(dens),
  +                "dens": dens,
  +            },
  +        )
  +
  +    den_name = normalize_den_name(name) if name else None
  +
  +    if action == "destroy":
  +        if not confirm_destroy:
  +            return _result(
  +                "operate_den_destroy",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error={
  +                    "kind": "safety_check",
  +                    "message": "Destroy requires explicit confirmation: set confirm_destroy=True",
  +                    "failing_step": "confirm",
  +                    "command": [],
  +                    "exit_code": None,
  +                    "timed_out": False,
  +                    "stdout": "",
  +                    "stderr": "",
  +                    "remediation": [
  +                        "Add confirm_destroy=True to the operate_den call.",
  +                        "This action cannot be undone.",
  +                    ],
  +                },
  +            )
  +        if not den_name:
  +            return _result(
  +                "operate_den_destroy",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error={
  +                    "kind": "invalid_input",
  +                    "message": "Destroy action requires a den name.",
  +                    "failing_step": "input_validation",
  +                    "command": [],
  +                    "exit_code": None,
  +                    "timed_out": False,
  +                    "stdout": "",
  +                    "stderr": "",
  +                    "remediation": ["Provide a den name for destruction."],
  +                },
  +            )
  +
  +        destroy_step = _run_step("sprite_destroy", sprite_command("destroy", den_name), cwd=PROJECT_DIR, timeout_s=60)
  +        steps.append(destroy_step)
  +        if not destroy_step["ok"]:
  +            return _result(
  +                "operate_den_destroy",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error=_build_error(
  +                    destroy_step,
  +                    f"Failed to destroy den {den_name}.",
  +                    ["Check sprite CLI access.", f"Verify den {den_name} exists."],
  +                ),
  +            )
  +
  +        return _result(
  +            "operate_den_destroy",
  +            True,
  +            steps=steps,
  +            data={
  +                "action": "destroy",
  +                "den_name": den_name,
  +            },
  +        )
  +
  +    if action == "status":
  +        if not den_name:
  +            return _result(
  +                "operate_den_status",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error={
  +                    "kind": "invalid_input",
  +                    "message": "Status action requires a den name.",
  +                    "failing_step": "input_validation",
  +                    "command": [],
  +                    "exit_code": None,
  +                    "timed_out": False,
  +                    "stdout": "",
  +                    "stderr": "",
  +                    "remediation": ["Provide a den name for status."],
  +                },
  +            )
  +        status_step = _run_step("sprite_url", sprite_command("url", den_name), cwd=PROJECT_DIR, timeout_s=30)
  +        steps.append(status_step)
  +        if not status_step["ok"]:
  +            return _result(
  +                "operate_den_status",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error=_build_error(
  +                    status_step,
  +                    f"Failed to get status for den {den_name}.",
  +                    ["Check sprite CLI access.", f"Verify den {den_name} exists."],
  +                ),
  +            )
  +        url = parse_sprite_url(status_step["stdout"])
  +        if not url:
  +            return _result(
  +                "operate_den_status",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error={
  +                    "kind": "parse_error",
  +                    "message": "Could not parse URL from sprite status output.",
  +                    "failing_step": "parse_url",
  +                    "command": status_step["command"],
  +                    "exit_code": status_step["exit_code"],
  +                    "timed_out": status_step["timed_out"],
  +                    "stdout": status_step["stdout"],
  +                    "stderr": status_step["stderr"],
  +                    "remediation": [
  +                        "Ensure sprite CLI output for `sprite url` is as expected."
  +                    ],
  +                },
  +            )
  +        return _result(
  +            "operate_den_status",
  +            True,
  +            steps=steps,
  +            data={
  +                "action": "status",
  +                "den_name": den_name,
  +                "url": url,
  +            },
  +        )
  +
  +    if action == "domain":
  +        if not den_name or not custom_domain:
  +            return _result(
  +                "operate_den_domain",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error={
  +                    "kind": "invalid_input",
  +                    "message": "Domain action requires a den name and custom_domain.",
  +                    "failing_step": "input_validation",
  +                    "command": [],
  +                    "exit_code": None,
  +                    "timed_out": False,
  +                    "stdout": "",
  +                    "stderr": "",
  +                    "remediation": [
  +                        "Provide both 'name' and 'custom_domain' parameters."
  +                    ],
  +                },
  +            )
  +        try:
  +            sesame_cmd = _sesame_command()
  +        except FileNotFoundError:
  +            return _result(
  +                "operate_den_domain",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error={
  +                    "kind": "missing_dependency",
  +                    "message": "sesame is required for custom domain management",
  +                    "failing_step": "preflight",
  +                    "command": ["sesame", "--help"],
  +                    "exit_code": None,
  +                    "timed_out": False,
  +                    "stdout": "",
  +                    "stderr": "sesame is not on PATH and no local build was found",
  +                    "remediation": [
  +                        "Build or install sesame.",
  +                    ],
  +                },
  +            )
  +
  +        # First ensure the sprite URL is public
  +        public_step = _run_step(
  +            "sprite_url_public",
  +            sprite_command("url", "update", "--auth", "public", sprite_name=den_name),
  +            cwd=PROJECT_DIR,
  +            timeout_s=30,
  +        )
  +        steps.append(public_step)
  +        if not public_step["ok"]:
  +            return _result(
  +                "operate_den_domain",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error=_build_error(
  +                    public_step,
  +                    "Failed to make the sprite URL public.",
  +                    ["Check sprite CLI access.", "Verify sprite is operational."],
  +                ),
  +            )
  +
  +        # Get the public sprite URL
  +        status_step = _run_step("sprite_url", sprite_command("url", den_name), cwd=PROJECT_DIR, timeout_s=30)
  +        steps.append(status_step)
  +        if not status_step["ok"]:
  +            return _result(
  +                "operate_den_domain",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error=_build_error(
  +                    status_step,
  +                    f"Failed to retrieve URL for den {den_name}.",
  +                    ["Check sprite CLI access.", f"Verify den {den_name} exists."],
  +                ),
  +            )
  +        target_url = parse_sprite_url(status_step["stdout"])
  +        if not target_url:
  +            return _result(
  +                "operate_den_domain",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error={
  +                    "kind": "parse_error",
  +                    "message": "Could not parse URL from sprite status output.",
  +                    "failing_step": "parse_target_url",
  +                    "command": status_step["command"],
  +                    "exit_code": status_step["exit_code"],
  +                    "timed_out": status_step["timed_out"],
  +                    "stdout": status_step["stdout"],
  +                    "stderr": status_step["stderr"],
  +                    "remediation": [
  +                        "Ensure sprite CLI output for `sprite url` is as expected."
  +                    ],
  +                },
  +            )
  +
  +        # Add URL forward via sesame
  +        domain_add_step = _run_step(
  +            "sesame_domain_add",
  +            _sesame_url_forward_command(custom_domain, target_url),
  +            cwd=None,
  +            timeout_s=30,
  +        )
  +        steps.append(domain_add_step)
  +        if not domain_add_step["ok"]:
  +            return _result(
  +                "operate_den_domain",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error=_build_error(
  +                    domain_add_step,
  +                    "Failed to create Porkbun URL forward via sesame.",
  +                    ["Check sesame configuration and API access.", "Verify custom domain ownership."],
  +                ),
  +            )
  +        return _result(
  +            "operate_den_domain",
  +            True,
  +            steps=steps,
  +            data={
  +                "action": "domain",
  +                "den_name": den_name,
  +                "custom_domain": custom_domain,
  +                "target_url": target_url,
  +            },
  +        )
  +
  +    if action in ("redeploy", "logs", "create"):
  +        return _result(
  +            f"operate_den_{action}",
  +            False,
  +            steps=steps,
  +            error={
  +                "kind": "unsupported_action",
  +                "message": f"Action '{action}' is not supported by the MCP operate_den tool directly.",
  +                "failing_step": "action_dispatch",
  +                "command": [],
  +                "exit_code": None,
  +                "timed_out": False,
  +                "stdout": "",
  +                "stderr": "",
  +                "remediation": [
  +                    "Use the CLI `den` command which implements these actions separately."
  +                ],
  +            },
  +        )
  +
  +    return _result(
  +        "operate_den_unknown",
  +        False,
  +        steps=steps,
  +        error={
  +            "kind": "invalid_action",
  +            "message": f"Unknown action: {action}",
  +            "failing_step": "action_dispatch",
  +            "command": [],
  +            "exit_code": None,
  +            "timed_out": False,
  +            "stdout": "",
  +            "stderr": "",
  +            "remediation": [
  +                "Provide a valid action for operate_den, such as 'list', 'destroy', 'status', 'domain'."
  +            ],
  +        },
  +    )
  +```
  +
  +#### diagnose_den
  +Runs a series of diagnostic checks on the Den environment to verify health and readiness, stopping on the first failure unless specified.
  +```python
  +@mcp.tool
  +def diagnose_den(include_docker_build: bool = False) -> dict[str, Any]:
  +    """Run diagnostic checks on den tooling and setup.\n\n    This is a quick way to verify that the CLI and its dependencies are working.
  +    """
  +    steps: list[StepResult] = []
  +
  +    # Define the diagnostic steps
  +    diagnostic_steps = [
  +        ("mypy", ["mypy", PROJECT_DIR], PROJECT_DIR, 300, "`mypy` checks failed.", ["Fix type errors in the project."]),
  +        ("property_tests", ["pytest", "-m", "properties", str(PROJECT_DIR)], PROJECT_DIR, 300, "Property tests failed.", ["Inspect test failures and fix."]),
  +        ("den_smoke", ["bash", "-lc", "den list"], PROJECT_DIR, 30, "Den smoke test failed (list command).", ["Check `den list` manually."]),
  +    ]
  +
  +    if include_docker_build:
  +        diagnostic_steps.append(
  +            ("den_full", ["bash", "-lc", "den build-image"], PROJECT_DIR, 900, "Den full build failed.", ["Inspect logs, fix build errors."])
  +        )
  +
  +    for step_name, command, cwd, timeout_s, error_msg, remediation in diagnostic_steps:
  +        step = _run_step(step_name, command, cwd=cwd, timeout_s=timeout_s)
  +        steps.append(step)
  +        if not step["ok"]:
  +            return _result(
  +                "diagnose_den",
  +                False,
  +                steps=steps,
  +                error=_build_error(step, error_msg, remediation),
  +            )
  +
  +    return _result(
  +        "diagnose_den",
  +        True,
  +        steps=steps,
  +        data={"message": "All diagnostic checks passed."},
  +        next_steps=["Your den environment is ready."],
  +    )
  +```
  +
  +## Module: `den_cli.cli`
  +
  +This module defines the command-line interface for `den_cli` using `typer`, providing user-facing commands for interacting with Den environments.
  +
  +### Classes & Enums (`den_cli.cli`)
  +
  +#### Backend (StrEnum)
  +An enumeration representing the supported Den backend types.
  +```python
  +class Backend(StrEnum):
  +    nix = "nix"
  +    guix = "guix"
  +```
  +
  +#### CommandError (Exception)
  +A custom exception `CommandError` raised when a shell command executed by the CLI fails.
  +```python
  +class CommandError(RuntimeError):
  +    pass
  +```
  +
  +### CLI Commands (`den_cli.cli`)
  +These functions are exposed as top-level commands via the `den` CLI application.
  +
  +#### setup
  +Infers a `den.dhall` configuration from a repository `path` and generates reproducible artifacts. Can `force` overwrite or `print_only` the result.
  +```python
  +@app.command()
  +def setup(
  +    path: Annotated[Path, typer.Argument(help="Repository path to inspect")] = Path("."),
  +    force: Annotated[bool, typer.Option("--force", help="Overwrite an existing den.dhall")] = False,
  +    print_only: Annotated[bool, typer.Option("--print", help="Print inferred den.dhall instead of writing files")] = False,
  +) -> None:
  +    """Infer `den.dhall` from a repository and generate reproducible artifacts.\n\n    The command inspects common project markers, chooses a backend heuristic,
  +    writes the inferred Dhall config, and then runs the Dhall generator script
  +    to materialize backend-specific files in the target repository.
  +    """
  +    repo_dir = path.resolve()
  +    if not repo_dir.is_dir():
  +        raise CommandError(f"Repository path not found: {repo_dir}")
  +    if not DHALL_DIR.is_dir():
  +        raise CommandError(f"Dhall templates not found at {DHALL_DIR}")
  +
  +    typer.secho(f"==> den setup {repo_dir}", fg=typer.colors.CYAN)
  +
  +    inferred = infer_den_setup(repo_dir)
  +    markers = detect_project_markers(repo_dir)
  +    rendered = render_den_dhall(inferred, DHALL_DIR)
  +
  +    typer.echo(f"  Name:       {inferred.name}")
  +    typer.echo(f"  Backend:    {inferred.backend}")
  +    typer.echo(f"  Dockerfile: {inferred.dockerfile or 'default'}")
  +    typer.echo("  Signals:")
  +    if inferred.reasons:
  +        for reason in inferred.reasons:
  +            typer.echo(f"    - {reason}")
  +    else:
  +        typer.echo("    - no strong signals detected")
  +
  +    detected_markers = {
  +        "package.json": markers.has_package_json,
  +        "bun.lock": markers.has_bun_lock,
  +        "pyproject.toml": markers.has_pyproject,
  +        "Cargo.toml": markers.has_cargo_toml,
  +        "Dockerfile/Containerfile": markers.has_dockerfile or markers.has_containerfile,
  +        "mise.toml": markers.has_mise_toml,
  +        "flox.toml": markers.has_flox_toml,
  +        "Helm chart": markers.has_helm_chart,
  +        "Guix manifest": markers.has_guix_manifest or markers.has_guix_channels,
  +        "Nix metadata": markers.has_nix_flake or markers.has_shell_nix,
  +    }
  +    for label, present in detected_markers.items():
  +        if present:
  +            typer.echo(f"    - detected {label}")
  +
  +    if print_only:
  +       ... (truncated)
  +```
  +
  +#### spawn
  +Provisions a new Den environment named `name`, optionally configuring `tailscale_authkey` and `custom_domain`. This command delegates to `mcp_server.provision_den`.
  +```python
  +@app.command()
  +def spawn(
  +    name: Annotated[str, typer.Argument(help="Name of the den")],
  +    backend: Annotated[Backend, typer.Option(help="Backend to use (nix/guix)")] = Backend.nix,
  +    tailscale_authkey: Annotated[str | None, typer.Option(help="Tailscale authkey for private networking")] = None,
  +    custom_domain: Annotated[str | None, typer.Option(help="Custom domain to attach to the den")] = None,
  +) -> None:
  +    """Provision a new den environment.\n\n    This creates a new Sprite, optionally configures Tailscale and a custom domain,
  +    and sets up basic services. This is a wrapper around `mcp_server.provision_den`.
  +    """
  +    typer.secho(f"==> Provisioning den {name}...", fg=typer.colors.CYAN)
  +    result = mcp_server.provision_den(
  +        name=name, backend=backend.value, tailscale_authkey=tailscale_authkey, custom_domain=custom_domain
  +    )
  +
  +    if result["ok"]:
  +        typer.secho(f"Den {name} provisioned successfully.", fg=typer.colors.GREEN)
  +        if url := result["data"].get("url"):
  +            typer.echo(f"Public URL: {url}")
  +        if custom_domain:
  +            typer.echo(f"Custom domain {custom_domain} configured.")
  +        _handle_mcp_output(result)
  +    else:
  +        typer.secho(f"Provisioning den {name} failed.", fg=typer.colors.RED)
  +        _handle_mcp_output(result)
  +        raise CommandError("Provisioning failed")
  +```
  +
  +#### destroy
  +Destroys a specified Den environment `name`. Requires explicit confirmation with `--yes`.
  +```python
  +@app.command()
  +def destroy(
  +    name: Annotated[str, typer.Argument(help="Name of the den to destroy")],
  +    yes: Annotated[bool, typer.Option("--yes", "-y", help="Confirm destruction")] = False,
  +) -> None:
  +    """Destroy a den environment.\n\n    This operation is irreversible.
  +    """
  +    typer.secho(f"==> Destroying den {name}...", fg=typer.colors.CYAN)
  +    result = mcp_server.operate_den(action="destroy", name=name, confirm_destroy=yes)
  +    _handle_mcp_output(result)
  +    if not result["ok"]:
  +        raise CommandError(f"Failed to destroy den {name}")
  +```
  +
  +#### use
  +Binds the current working directory to a specific Den identified by `name`, allowing subsequent commands to target it implicitly.
  +```python
  +@app.command()
  +def use(
  +    name: Annotated[str | None, typer.Argument(help="Name of the den to bind to")] = None,
  +) -> None:
  +    """Bind current directory to a den."
  +    _ensure_project_dir()
  +    den_name = name or _choose_den_name("Bind current directory to")
  +    typer.secho(f"==> Binding to den {den_name}...", fg=typer.colors.CYAN)
  +    _run_checked(sprite_use_command(den_name), cwd=PROJECT_DIR)
  +    typer.secho(f"Successfully bound to den {den_name}", fg=typer.colors.GREEN)
  +```
  +
  +#### exec
  +Executes a `command` inside a specified Den `name`, either interactively (`--tty`) or non-interactively. Additional arguments are passed directly to the command.
  +```python
  +@app.command(
  +    context_settings={"allow_extra_args": True, "ignore_unknown_options": True},
  +)
  +def exec(
  +    name: Annotated[str, typer.Argument(help="Name of the den")],
  +    command: Annotated[list[str], typer.Argument(help="Command and its arguments to run inside the den")],
  +    tty: Annotated[bool, typer.Option("--tty", help="Connect a TTY for interactive execution")] = False,
  +) -> None:
  +    """Execute a command inside a den.\n\n    Example: `den exec myproject ls -l /`\n    """
  +    _ensure_project_dir()
  +    if not command:
  +        raise CommandError("Provide a command to run inside the den.")
  +    den_name = normalize_den_name(name)
  +    sprite_cmd = sprite_tty_exec_command(den_name, command) if tty else sprite_exec_command(den_name, command)
  +    _run_checked(sprite_cmd, cwd=PROJECT_DIR, capture_output=False)
  +```
  +
  +#### logs
  +Manages and views logs/sessions for a Den `name`. Can `list_only` available sessions or `selector` to attach to a specific one.
  +```python
  +@app.command()
  +def logs(
  +    name: Annotated[str, typer.Argument(help="Name of the den")],
  +    selector: Annotated[str | None, typer.Argument(help="Session ID to attach to, or omitted to list sessions")] = None,
  +    list_only: Annotated[bool, typer.Option("--list", "-l", help="List active sessions only")] = False,
  +) -> None:
  +    """List or attach to den sessions."
  +    _ensure_project_dir()
  +    den_name = normalize_den_name(name)
  +
  +    typer.secho(f"==> Den logs for {den_name}...", fg=typer.colors.CYAN)
  +    command = sprite_logs_command(den_name, selector, list_only=list_only)
  +    _run_checked(command, cwd=PROJECT_DIR, capture_output=False)
  +```
  +
  +#### redeploy
  +Triggers a redeployment of a Den `name` by creating a checkpoint and then restoring it.
  +```python
  +@app.command()
  +def redeploy(
  +    name: Annotated[str, typer.Argument(help="Name of the den")],
  +) -> None:
  +    """Create a checkpoint and restore it, forcing a redeploy.\n\n    This is useful for applying configuration changes or restarting a stuck den.
  +    """
  +    _ensure_project_dir()
  +    den_name = normalize_den_name(name)
  +    typer.secho(f"==> Redeploying den {den_name}...", fg=typer.colors.CYAN)
  +
  +    nonce = str(time.time_ns())
  +    comment = make_sprite_redeploy_comment(den_name, nonce)
  +
  +    # Create a new checkpoint
  +    _run_checked(
  +        sprite_checkpoint_create_command(den_name, comment),
  +        cwd=PROJECT_DIR,
  +        error_hint="Checkpoint creation failed.",
  +    )
  +
  +    # Find the version ID of the newly created checkpoint
  +    # First try API, then fallback to list output
  +    version_id = None
  +    proc_api = _run(sprite_command("api", "/checkpoints", sprite_name=den_name), capture_output=True)
  +    if proc_api.returncode == 0:
  +        version_id = find_checkpoint_version_in_api_output(proc_api.stdout, comment)
  +    if version_id is None:
  +        proc_list = _run(sprite_command("checkpoint", "list", sprite_name=den_name), capture_output=True)
  +        if proc_list.returncode == 0:
  +            version_id = find_checkpoint_version_in_list_output(proc_list.stdout, comment)
  +
  +    if not version_id:
  +        raise CommandError(f"Failed to find newly created checkpoint for {den_name}")
  +
  +    # Restore to the new checkpoint
  +    _run_checked(
  +        sprite_restore_command(den_name, version_id),
  +        cwd=PROJECT_DIR,
  +        error_hint=f"Checkpoint restore to {version_id} failed.",
  +    )
  +
  +    typer.secho(f"Den {den_name} redeployed successfully to version {version_id}.", fg=typer.colors.GREEN)
  +```
  +
  +#### status
  +Retrieves and displays the status of a specific Den `name`, including its public URL. This command delegates to `mcp_server.operate_den`.
  +```python
  +@app.command()
  +def status(
  +    name: Annotated[str, typer.Argument(help="Name of the den")],
  +) -> None:
  +    """Get the status of a den environment.\n\n    This includes its public URL and other relevant information.
  +    """
  +    _ensure_project_dir()
  +    typer.secho(f"==> Status for den {name}...", fg=typer.colors.CYAN)
  +    result = mcp_server.operate_den(action="status", name=name)
  +    _handle_mcp_output(result)
  +    if not result["ok"]:
  +        raise CommandError(f"Failed to get status for den {name}")
  +    if url := result["data"].get("url"):
  +        typer.echo(f"Public URL: {url}")
  +    else:
  +        typer.secho("No public URL found.", fg=typer.colors.YELLOW)
  +```
  +
  +#### domain
  +Attaches a `custom_domain` to a Den `name`, configuring it via `sesame`. This command delegates to `mcp_server.operate_den`.
  +```python
  +@app.command()
  +def domain(
  +    name: Annotated[str, typer.Argument(help="Name of the den")],
  +    custom_domain: Annotated[str, typer.Argument(help="Custom domain to attach to the den")],
  +) -> None:
  +    """Attach a custom domain to a den.\n\n    Requires `sesame` CLI to be installed and configured.
  +    """
  +    _ensure_project_dir()
  +    typer.secho(f"==> Attaching custom domain {custom_domain} to den {name}...", fg=typer.colors.CYAN)
  +    result = mcp_server.operate_den(action="domain", name=name, custom_domain=custom_domain)
  +    _handle_mcp_output(result)
  +    if not result["ok"]:
  +        raise CommandError(f"Failed to attach custom domain {custom_domain} to den {name}")
  +    typer.secho(f"Custom domain {custom_domain} successfully attached to den {name}.", fg=typer.colors.GREEN)
  +```
  +
  +#### diagnose
  +Runs diagnostic checks on the Den CLI environment and configured Dens. This command delegates to `mcp_server.diagnose_den`.
  +```python
  +@app.command()
  +def diagnose(
  +    include_docker_build: Annotated[bool, typer.Option("--include-docker-build", help="Include Docker build in diagnostics")] = False,
  +) -> None:
  +    """Run diagnostic checks.\n\n    Verifies local tooling, connectivity, and optionally, den image builds.
  +    """
  +    _ensure_project_dir()
  +    typer.secho("==> Running diagnostics...", fg=typer.colors.CYAN)
  +    result = mcp_server.diagnose_den(include_docker_build=include_docker_build)
  +    _handle_mcp_output(result)
  +    if not result["ok"]:
  +        raise CommandError("Diagnostic checks failed")
  +```
  +
  +#### provision
  +Provisions a new Den named `name`. This is an alias for `spawn` and also delegates to `mcp_server.provision_den`.
  +```python
  +@app.command()
  +def provision(
  +    name: Annotated[str, typer.Argument(help="Name of the den")],
  +    backend: Annotated[Backend, typer.Option(help="Backend to use (nix/guix)")] = Backend.nix,
  +    tailscale_authkey: Annotated[str | None, typer.Option(help="Tailscale authkey for private networking")] = None,
  +    custom_domain: Annotated[str | None, typer.Option(help="Custom domain to attach to the den")] = None,
  +) -> None:
  +    """Provision a new den environment. Alias for `spawn`."
  +    spawn(name, backend, tailscale_authkey, custom_domain)
  +```
  +
  +#### list-dens
  +Lists all currently managed Den environments. This command delegates to `mcp_server.operate_den` with the 'list' action.
  +```python
  +@app.command("list") # Renamed from `list_dens` for CLI
  +def list_dens() -> None:
  +    """List all active den environments."
  +    _ensure_project_dir()
  +    typer.secho("==> Listing dens...", fg=typer.colors.CYAN)
  +    result = mcp_server.operate_den(action="list")
  +    _handle_mcp_output(result)
  +    if not result["ok"]:
  +        raise CommandError("Failed to list dens")
  +    dens = result["data"].get("dens", [])
  +    if dens:
  +        typer.secho("Found dens:", fg=typer.colors.GREEN)
  +        for den in dens:
  +            typer.echo(f"- {den}")
  +    else:
  +        typer.secho("No dens found.", fg=typer.colors.YELLOW)
  +```
